<ol><li> Adagio - Allegro con brio (E<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>&#160;major)
</li><li> Adagio cantabile (A<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>&#160;major)
</li><li> Tempo di menuetto - Trio (E<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>&#160;major)
</li><li> Tema con variazioni. Andante (B<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>&#160;major)
</li><li> Scherzo. Allegro molto e vivace - Trio (E<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>&#160;major)
</li><li> Andante con molto alla marcia - Presto (E<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>&#160;major)
</li></ol>
</td></tr>
